<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Helping You walk the Camino de Santiago &amp; explore the world at a slower pace</h1>



<p class="has-text-align-left" style="margin-right:0;margin-left:0">I created&nbsp;<em>Then We Walked</em>&nbsp;for people like us — those who are:</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Looking For Camino or Travel Inspiration?</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">You&#8217;ll find oodles of content from our walking guides, travel tips, itineraries and stories — start with the Camino de Santiago or dive right into our slow travel adventures.</p>

<div class="wp-block-group is-layout-constrained wp-container-core-group-is-layout-d46ca558 wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;padding-top:0;padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);padding-bottom:0;padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30)">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading">I’m Colleen – Nice to Meet You!</h2>



<p>If you’re wondering who’s behind all this, and why you should listen to us, here’s my story &#8211; I’m Colleen, and I&#8217;m an English woman living in France.</p>



<p>I discovered the Camino in 2013, and after recovering from cancer, I walked 800 kilometres solo across Spain — and it changed my life. Since then, I’ve walked 22 Caminos (and counting), started a walking club, trained as a Lowland Leader with the British Mountaineering Association, volunteered in the Pilgrim Office and albergues and guided hundreds of new pilgrims along the Camino.</p>



<p>Since 2022, when Gerry and I retired, we’ve been on a mission to wander our way around the world — walking where we can, travelling slowly and creating our own stories along the way.</p>



<p>If you dream of exploring distant shores or walking your own Camino, you’re in the right place. Here we share our itineraries, experiences and the lessons we’ve learned along the way.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-gallery has-nested-images columns-default is-cropped wp-block-gallery-1 is-layout-flex wp-block-gallery-is-layout-flex" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30)">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Looking for ideas to spark your next adventure?</h2>



<p>These are the guides that our readers return to again and again — from step-by-step Camino walking routes and stages to a few of our unforgettable slow travel experiences. </p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">We Retired. Now We’re Walking and Travelling the World</h2>



<p>We’ve called France home for almost 20 years, but our love of walking and slow travel keeps pulling us to new places. </p>



<p>These days your 50s are the new 30s, and your 60s are just the start of the next adventure!  We waited half a lifetime to get started but as a wise young Bedouin once told me in Dana in Jordan: <em>every sunrise is a new opportunity.</em></p>



<p>We’re always on the move — here’s where you’ll find our most recent adventures.</p>
